The ranking of the cards in this deck are as follows (from high to low); Ace, King, Queen, Jack, 10, 9, 8, 7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 2. \r\n\r\nThe player who draws the highest card of all would be designated the first dealer. \r\n\r\nThe dealer shuffles the cards and deals the hand. If no trump card has been played to the trick, the highest card of the suit led wins the trick. The winner of each trick leads the first card to the next trick.
